(*************************************************************************

 Every adjunction gives rise to a monad

 In arbitrary bicategories, every adjunction gives rise to a monad

 *************************************************************************)

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Categories.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.Bicat. Import Bicat.Notations.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.BicategoryLaws.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.Invertible_2cells.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Core.Unitors.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.Morphisms.Adjunctions.
Require Import UniMath.Bicategories.DisplayedBicats.Examples.MonadsLax.

Local Open Scope cat.

Section MonadFromAdjunction.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {x y : B}
          (l : adjunction x y).

  Let r : y --> x := left_adjoint_right_adjoint l.
  Let Œ∑ : id‚ÇÅ _ ==> l ¬∑ r := left_adjoint_unit l.
  Let Œµ : r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ _ := left_adjoint_counit l.

  Let f : x --> x := l ¬∑ r.
  Let monad_Œ∑ : id‚ÇÅ _ ==> f := Œ∑.
  Let monad_Œº : f ¬∑ f ==> f
    := rassociator _ _ _
       ‚Ä¢ (_ ‚óÉ lassociator _ _ _)
       ‚Ä¢ (_ ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ _))
       ‚Ä¢ (_ ‚óÉ lunitor _).

  
B: bicat
x, y: B
l: adjunction x y
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint l: B ‚ü¶ y, x ‚üß
Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r
Œµ:= left_adjoint_counit l: r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ y
f:= l ¬∑ r: B ‚ü¶ x, x ‚üß
monad_Œ∑:= Œ∑: id‚ÇÅ x ==> f
monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
(linvunitor f ‚Ä¢ (monad_Œ∑ ‚ñπ f)) ‚Ä¢ monad_Œº = id‚ÇÇ f

Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r
Œµ:= left_adjoint_counit l: r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ y
f:= l ¬∑ r: B ‚ü¶ x, x ‚üß
monad_Œ∑:= Œ∑: id‚ÇÅ x ==> f
monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
p‚ÇÅ: linvunitor l
‚Ä¢ ((left_adjoint_unit l ‚ñπ l)
   ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l
        (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l) l
      ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ left_adjoint_counit l) ‚Ä¢ runitor l))) =
id‚ÇÇ l
((Œ∑ ‚ñπ l) ‚ñπ r)
‚Ä¢ (rassociator (l ¬∑ r) l r
   ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
      ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)
         ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r)) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r))))) =
((left_adjoint_unit l ‚ñπ l) ‚ñπ r)
‚Ä¢ ((rassociator l (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l) l ‚ñπ r)
   ‚Ä¢ (((l ‚óÉ left_adjoint_counit l) ‚ñπ r)
      ‚Ä¢ (runitor l ‚ñπ r)))

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r

  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
(rinvunitor f ‚Ä¢ (f ‚óÉ monad_Œ∑)) ‚Ä¢ monad_Œº = id‚ÇÇ f

B: bicat
x, y: B
l: adjunction x y
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint l: B ‚ü¶ y, x ‚üß
Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r
Œµ:= left_adjoint_counit l: r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ y
f:= l ¬∑ r: B ‚ü¶ x, x ‚üß
monad_Œ∑:= Œ∑: id‚ÇÅ x ==> f
monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
p‚ÇÅ:= internal_triangle1 l: (((linvunitor l ‚Ä¢ (left_adjoint_unit l ‚ñπ l))
  ‚Ä¢ rassociator l (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
      l) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ left_adjoint_counit l))
‚Ä¢ runitor l = id‚ÇÇ l
p‚ÇÇ: rinvunitor (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
‚Ä¢ ((left_adjoint_right_adjoint l
    ‚óÉ left_adjoint_unit l)
   ‚Ä¢ (lassociator (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
        l (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
      ‚Ä¢ ((left_adjoint_counit l
          ‚ñπ left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
         ‚Ä¢ lunitor (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)))) =
id‚ÇÇ (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l)
(l ‚óÉ rinvunitor (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l))
‚Ä¢ ((l
    ‚óÉ (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l
       ‚óÉ left_adjoint_unit l))
   ‚Ä¢ ((l
       ‚óÉ lassociator (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l) l
           (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l))
      ‚Ä¢ ((l
          ‚óÉ (left_adjoint_counit l
             ‚ñπ left_adjoint_right_adjoint l))
         ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor (left_adjoint_right_adjoint l))))) =
((l ‚óÉ rinvunitor r) ‚Ä¢ lassociator l r (id‚ÇÅ x))
‚Ä¢ ((l ¬∑ r ‚óÉ Œ∑)
   ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
      ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)
         ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r)) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r)))))

B: bicat
x, y: B
l: adjunction x y
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint l: B ‚ü¶ y, x ‚üß
Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r
Œµ:= left_adjoint_counit l: r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ y
f:= l ¬∑ r: B ‚ü¶ x, x ‚üß
monad_Œ∑:= Œ∑: id‚ÇÅ x ==> f
monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
(rassociator f f f ‚Ä¢ (f ‚óÉ monad_Œº)) ‚Ä¢ monad_Œº =
(monad_Œº ‚ñπ f) ‚Ä¢ monad_Œº

 ‚Ä¢ rassociator l (id‚ÇÅ y) (id‚ÇÅ y ¬∑ r))
‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (id‚ÇÅ y ‚óÉ lunitor r)) = ?t2

monad_Œ∑:= Œ∑: id‚ÇÅ x ==> f
monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
rassociator f f f
‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r))
   ‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r))
      ‚Ä¢ (lassociator (l ¬∑ r) l (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)
         ‚Ä¢ ((rassociator l r l ‚ñπ r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)
            ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l (r ¬∑ l) (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)
               ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r))
                  ‚Ä¢ (l
                     ‚óÉ ((lunitor (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r) ‚Ä¢ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))
                        ‚Ä¢ lunitor r)))))))) =
(rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r) ‚ñπ f)
‚Ä¢ (((l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r) ‚ñπ f)
   ‚Ä¢ (((l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r)) ‚ñπ f)
      ‚Ä¢ (((l ‚óÉ lunitor r) ‚ñπ f)
         ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
            ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)
               ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r)) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r)))))))

      ‚Ä¢ (f ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)))
     ‚Ä¢ lassociator (l ¬∑ r) l (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r))
    ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l r l ‚ñπ r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r))
   ‚Ä¢ rassociator l (r ¬∑ l) (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r))
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)))
 ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator (id‚ÇÅ y) (r ¬∑ l) r))
‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (lassociator (id‚ÇÅ y) r l ‚ñπ r))

         ‚Ä¢ ((rassociator l r l ‚ñπ r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)
            ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l (r ¬∑ l) (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)
               ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ lassociator (r ¬∑ l) (r ¬∑ l) r)
                  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (lassociator (r ¬∑ l) r l ‚ñπ r)))))))) =
(rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r) ‚ñπ f)
‚Ä¢ (((l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r) ‚ñπ f)
   ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r) (l ¬∑ r)
      ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r) l r)))

 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
((((rassociator f f f ‚Ä¢ (f ‚óÉ rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)))
   ‚Ä¢ (f ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)))
  ‚Ä¢ rassociator l r (l ¬∑ (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r)))
 ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (r ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ rassociator r l r))))
‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (r ‚óÉ lassociator l r (l ¬∑ r))) =
rassociator (l ¬∑ r) f f ‚Ä¢ rassociator l r (f ¬∑ f)

monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f

‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r))
   ‚Ä¢ ((f ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r))
      ‚Ä¢ (rassociator l r (l ¬∑ (r ¬∑ l ¬∑ r))
         ‚Ä¢ ((l ‚óÉ (r ‚óÉ (l ‚óÉ rassociator r l r)))
            ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ (r ‚óÉ lassociator l r (l ¬∑ r))))))) =
rassociator (l ¬∑ r) f f ‚Ä¢ rassociator l r (f ¬∑ f)

(rinvunitor (pr12 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº))
 ‚Ä¢ (pr12 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº)
    ‚óÉ pr122 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº)))

id‚ÇÇ (pr12 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº))
 exact mnd_from_adjunction_Œ∑_right.
      
B: bicat
x, y: B
l: adjunction x y
r:= left_adjoint_right_adjoint l: B ‚ü¶ y, x ‚üß
Œ∑:= left_adjoint_unit l: id‚ÇÅ x ==> l ¬∑ r
Œµ:= left_adjoint_counit l: r ¬∑ l ==> id‚ÇÅ y
f:= l ¬∑ r: B ‚ü¶ x, x ‚üß

monad_Œº:= ((rassociator l r (l ¬∑ r)
  ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lassociator r l r)) ‚Ä¢ 
 (l ‚óÉ (Œµ ‚ñπ r))) ‚Ä¢ (l ‚óÉ lunitor r): f ¬∑ f ==> f
(rassociator
   (pr12 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº))

      (pr1 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº),,

   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº),,

 ‚Ä¢ (pr12 (make_mnd_data x f monad_Œ∑ monad_Œº)

 exact mnd_from_adjunction_assoc.

End MonadFromAdjunction.
